
Separate embeddings for query and story, concatenated along the embedding dimension, and fed into LSTM based encoder with output generated using softmax.
Baseline model with strong supervision performed very well on some of the tasks whereas model with weak supervision was almost at par with Facebook and Keras based similar LSTM/GRU based models.
Baseline model performed poorly on tasks containing many & long sentences and answer needing transitive inference & temporal order.


Question Answering:
advanced models:
1. memnn: https://github.com/domluna/memn2n
2. QRN: https://github.com/yfletberliac/Mango Query-Reduction Network character-level RNN
3. Dynamic memory network
